msg:TEDA International Hotel
Come to Binhai and book the TEDA International Hotel through Xcheng. It is next to the International Shopping Center. There are also many parking spaces.

There is a large outdoor courtyard, fountains, corridors, gardens... A relatively "traditional" high-end hotel with a retro style... The first floor of the hotel is also a traditional garden style, surrounded by rooms and a high and deep patio.

The hotel rooms are also very large, especially the suites, which are very cost-effective. The bed is a 2-meter big bed. The settings are relatively complete. However, the last renovation of the entire hotel should be in 2013, so it looks a bit old, which is also the hotel's flaw.

The service is also very enthusiastic.

It is a good choice for family travel, and the cost-effectiveness will be relatively high.

name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Superior Suite
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.3
posted:Posted April 14, 2024
msg:The accommodation experience this time was pretty good. Whether it was the environment or the room decoration, it was definitely a five-star hotel. It's just that after a long time, some facilities can still be used, but they still leave traces of time. The whole hotel gave me the feeling of an old nobleman submerged by the times. It may not be so new and avant-garde, but the years of heritage allow the guests staying here to still experience a different kind of humanistic feelings.
A hotel's facilities and environment will always age after years of erosion. Only sincere service will always be the magic weapon to retain guests. The service staff here are completely free of the kind of programmed cold politeness, and of course not the kind of embarrassing enthusiasm. They can always find a balance between the two. For example, when I asked to take half a cup of hot water with my child's water cup, they would take the initiative to ask if I wanted to drink warm water immediately. After getting my confirmation, they would pour some of the diluted water on the back of their hands to test the water temperature. When I said that the socket in the room seemed to be out of power, they would ask if it was convenient to go into the room now to check, and after checking, they would take the initiative to find me in the restaurant to explain the reason to me, even if the power outage was due to my operating error.
The staff here really seem to treat this hotel as their own home, and everyone is sincerely willing to do something for this home. If this is trained, I can only say that it deserves to be a five-star hotel...
Finally, to the travelers who come here, if you come to stay here, forget the star rating first. The facilities may be old, but the hygiene is absolutely fine, and the service is really great!!!
